Tyrsenian , named after the Tyrrhenians , is a proposed extinct family of closely related ancient languages put forward by linguist Helmut Rix , which consists of the Etruscan language of northern, central and south-western Italy, and eastern Corsica ; the Rhaetic language of the Alps, named after the Rhaetian people; and the Lemnian language of the Aegean Sea.
